***kleed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleed.html>kleed</a> (2433)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clêet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klēth</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klaiþą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kleid</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleed.html>Kleed</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cloth</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cleie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:klei.html>klei</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klajjaz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gley-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to glue, stick together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***kleingeestig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleingeestig.html>kleingeestig</a> (47096)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Mid to late eighteenth century. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>geest</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kleingeistig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleingeestig.html>kleingeestig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleingeestig.html>kleingeestiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">kleingeestigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>narrow-minded, prejudiced
<ul><li><b>1788</b>, Elisabeth <a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> Post, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, in <a href = vnd.unilang:brieven.html>brieven</a></i>, publ. by <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> Allart (third print), page 72.

***kleinzerig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleinzerig.html>kleinzerig</a> (54110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hurt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleinzerig.html>kleinzerig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleinzerig.html>kleinzeriger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">kleinzerigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>petty in relation to pain or hardship, with a low pain threshold, with little endurance</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***klemmen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klemmen.html>klemmen</a> (26175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clemmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:klemmen.html>klemmen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klamjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klemmen.html>klemmen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to clamp, to squeeze</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to jam, to not move smoothly</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cleppe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rattle used by <a href = vnd.unilang:leep.html>lepers</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***klere.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klere.html>klere</a> (2956)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kolere.html>kolere</a></i>, formerly also spelled <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">colère</i>. The modern Dutch term for the disease <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cholera.html>cholera</a></i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clēricus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a priest, clergyman, cleric, also generally a learned <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, clerk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κληρικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klērikós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(adj. in church jargon) of the clergy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλῆρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klêros</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lot, inheritance,” originally “a shard used in casting lots</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***kletskop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kletskop.html>kletskop</a> (64415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Glatzkopf</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">baldie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Glatze</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bald head;</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kopf</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kletskop.html>kletskop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kletskoppen.html>kletskoppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kletskop.html>kletskopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bald head.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bald person (usually <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> of a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>), a baldie.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kaalkop</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kale.html>kale</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A hard and brittle type of cookie, with sugar, butter and <a href = vnd.unilang:peanuts.html>peanuts</a> or almonds as main ingredients.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***kleven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleven</a> (21308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clēven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">clivon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klibāną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gleybʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stick, to be attached glue-like
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ineens.html>Ineens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:merkte.html>merkte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kauwgom.html>kauwgom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sandaal.html>sandaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleefde.html>kleefde</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Suddenly she noticed that there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> chewing gum <b>sticking</b> to her sandal.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to glue, to adhere something on/to something else, to stick to/on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaagt.html>plaagt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> kauwgum <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snor.html>snor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleven</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> teasing her dad by <b>sticking</b> chewing gum on his moustache.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be sticky
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grondstof.html>grondstof</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleeft.html>kleeft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This resource <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> very very <b>sticky</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/road_transport" class="extiw" title="w:road transport">road transport</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tailgate (drive dangerously close)

***klikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klikken.html>klikken</a> (11310)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clicken</i>, of imitative origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klikken.html>klikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to click</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go well relationwise, to have a click</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to squeal on someone, to snitch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall into place mentally <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">as in <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">the <a href = vnd.unilang:penny.html>penny</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drops.html>drops</a></i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***kliko.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kliko.html>kliko</a> (116078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href = vnd.unilang:kliko.html>Kliko</a>, acronym of proper names Klinkenberg and <a href = vnd.unilang:koster.html>Koster</a>, a company that historically <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wheelie.html>wheelie</a> bins.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kliko.html>kliko</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kliko.html>kliko</a>'s</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:wheelie.html>wheelie</a> bin (outdoor tall plastic garbage container with two <a href = vnd.unilang:wheels.html>wheels</a> to one side)</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">minicontainer</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">sulo</span> (regional)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">milko</span> (regional)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:otto.html>otto</a></span> (regional)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>engels</a></span> (regional)</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">climat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clima</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλίμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klíma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inclination</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλίνω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klínō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:slopen.html>slope</a>, incline</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from which also <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cline</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱley-</i> (English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lean</i>).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klimaatregeling.html>klimaatregeling</a> (82136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klimaat.html>klimaat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regeling.html>regeling</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">climate control</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klimop.html>klimop</a> (34121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opklimmen.html>opklimmen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to climb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>ivy (plant), <i>Hedera helix</i></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klinker.html>klinker</a> (34119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">klinkaerd</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinken.html>klinken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinker.html>klinker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinkers.html>klinkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinker.html>klinkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>clinker brick; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of brick used for pavement</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">klinkerweg</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinken.html>klinken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vocālis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinker.html>klinker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinkers.html>klinkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinker.html>klinkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> vowel

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clippe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klippa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klippō</i>.
